<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 dances:
<ol><li> Joc cu bâtǎ. Allegro moderato
</li><li> Brâul. Allegro
</li><li> Pê-loc. Andante
</li><li> Buciumeana. Moderato
</li><li> Poargǎ româneascǎ. Allegro
</li><li> Mǎrunţel. Allegro
</li></ol>
